Gayatri Projects Limited    GAYAPROJ : Cessation GAYAPROJ : Gayatri Projects Limited has informed the Exchange regarding Cessation of Mr Birendra Kumar as Nominee Director of the company w.e.f. May 18, 2020.

Pursuant to the provisions of Regulation 30 of the SEBI (Listing Obligation & Disclosure Requirements) Regulations, 2015, we are wish to inform that Bank of Baroda (Lead Banker of the Consortium) has withdrawn the nomination of Mr. Birendra Kumar (DIN: 08071170) as its nominee on the Board of Directors of the Company, vide their letter dated May 18, 2020 (Letter Attached as Annexure - II). The said letter has been received by the Company on May 19, 2020. Accordingly, Mr. Birendra Kumar, Nominee Director, ceases to be director on the Board of Directors of the Company.

As per the terms of the loan documentation, the Lead Banker i.e Bank of Baroda will appoint a new nominee director in due course.

Disclosure with regard to change in Director is attached as Annexure I.
